<script
type="text/javascript">










amznJQ.onReady('jQuery',
function()
{








var
attachEntityAlert
=
function()
{












var
entityAlertContainer
=
jQuery('#entity-alert');












var
entityAlertSavingMsg
=
entityAlertContainer.find('.saving-action');













entityAlertContainer.find(".entity-alert-body.subscription-action").each(function()
{
















var
currentMessage
=
jQuery(this);
















var
subscriptionAction
=
currentMessage.find(".subscription-action");

















var
url,
eventToBind;
















if
(subscriptionAction.attr('href'))
{




















url
=
subscriptionAction.attr("href");




















eventToBind
=
'click';
















}
else
if
(subscriptionAction.attr('action'))
{




















var
url
=
subscriptionAction.attr("action");




















eventToBind
=
'submit';
















}
else
{




















return;
















}

















var
ajaxHandlerUrl
=
"/gp/entity-alert/external/entity-alert-subscription-ajax-handler.html";

















var
urlParts
=
url.split('?');
















var
urlParts2
=
urlParts[0].split("/ref=");
















var
params
=
"";

















if
(urlParts2.length
>
1)
{




















ajaxHandlerUrl
+=
"/ref="
+
urlParts2[1];
















}
















if
(urlParts.length
>
1)
{




















params=
urlParts[1];
















}

















var
currentState
=
currentMessage.attr('class').replace('entity-alert-body',
'');

















subscriptionAction.bind(eventToBind,
function()
{




















jQuery.ajax({
























url:
ajaxHandlerUrl,
























async:
true,
























type:
"POST",
























dataType:
"json",
























cache:
false,
























data:
params,
























beforeSend:
function()
{




























//
Also
explicitly
alter
the
CSS
because
the
style
for
detail
page
widget
is
all
inlined




























currentMessage.removeClass("show").css("display",
"none");




























entityAlertSavingMsg.addClass("show").css("display",
"block");
























},
























success:
function(data,
textStatus)
{




























if
(data.redirect)
{
































window.location.href
=
data.redirect;




























}
else
{
































var
newState
=
data.subscriptionState;
































//
Also
explicitly
alter
the
CSS
because
the
style
for
detail
page
widget
is
all
inlined
































entityAlertSavingMsg.removeClass("show").css("display",
"none");
































entityAlertContainer.find("."
+
newState).addClass("show").css("display",
"block");




























}
























},
























error:
function(data,
textStatus,
errorThrown)
{




























var
newState;





























if
(currentMessage.hasClass('not-subscribed')
||
currentMessage.hasClass('not-signed-in'))
{
































newState
=
'error-subscribe';




























}
else
if
(currentMessage.hasClass('subscribed'))
{
































newState
=
'error-unsubscribe';




























}
else
{
































newState
=
'generic-error';




























}





























//
Also
explicitly
alter
the
CSS
because
the
style
for
detail
page
widget
is
all
inlined




























entityAlertSavingMsg.removeClass("show").css("display",
"none");




























entityAlertContainer.find("."
+
newState).addClass("show").css("display",
"block");
























}




















});




















return
false;
















});












});








};








attachEntityAlert();




});

</script>

<script
type="text/javascript">
amznJQ.onReady('jQuery',
function
()
{

var
retriedCreateMp3Interface
=
false;
var
createMp3Interface
=
function($)
{
try
{




var
swfURL
=
"http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/zeitgeist/mp3player/swf/zgMp3Player-1.0._V212274098_.swf";




var
mp3PlayerElemId
=
"mp3FlashPlayer";




var
playerHeight
=
1;
//
should
be
1.

Flash
objects
initiated
with
0
dimensions
will
not
get
initialized




var
playerWidth
=
1;

//
should
be
1
as
well.




var
minFlashVersion
=
"9.0.0";




var
expressInstallSwfurl
=
null;

//
not
used




var
flashVars
=
{






protocol:
window.location.protocol.replace(":",""),






sessionId:
"187-2699161-3328836"
//
used
for
telemetry
logging




};




var
params
=
{






allowScriptAccess:
"always"
//
allow
JavaScript
to
call
the
MP3
player




};





if
(jQuery("#"
+
mp3PlayerElemId).length
===
0)
{








if
(jQuery(".mp3Player:first").length
!==
0)
{












jQuery(".mp3Player:first").append('<div
id="'
+
mp3PlayerElemId
+
'"></div>');








}
else
{












jQuery("body").append('<div
id="'
+
mp3PlayerElemId
+
'"></div>');








}




}





try
{








var
flashVersion
=
swfobject.getFlashPlayerVersion();




}
catch
(e)
{








//swfobject
not
defined








return;




}





swfobject.embedSWF(swfURL,
mp3PlayerElemId,
playerHeight,
playerWidth,
minFlashVersion,
expressInstallSwfurl,
flashVars,
params);





if
(!window.Mp3Interface)
{








window.Mp3Interface
=
{












flashPlayerId:
mp3PlayerElemId,












playerList:
[],












currentPlayer:
null,












muted:
false,












initialized:
false,












retriedInit:
false,














registerPlayer:
function(player)
{
















Mp3Interface.playerList.push(player);

















if
(Mp3Interface.currentPlayer
===
null
||
Mp3Interface.currentPlayer
===
undefined)
{




















Mp3Interface.currentPlayer
=
player;
















}

















if
(this.initialized)
{




















player.callback('onPlayerInit');
















}












},














playSong:
function(url,
requestingPlayer)
{
















Mp3Interface.setCurrentPlayer(requestingPlayer);
















try
{


















swfobject.getObjectById(Mp3Interface.flashPlayerId).playSong(url);
















}
catch
(e)
{


















return;
















}












},












playSongAsin:
function(asin,
realm,
requestingPlayer)
{
















Mp3Interface.setCurrentPlayer(requestingPlayer);
















try
{


















swfobject.getObjectById(Mp3Interface.flashPlayerId).playSongAsin(asin,
realm);
















}
catch
(e)
{


















return;
















}












},












pauseSong:
function(requestingPlayer)
{
















if
(requestingPlayer)
{




















Mp3Interface.setCurrentPlayer(requestingPlayer);
















}
















try
{


















swfobject.getObjectById(Mp3Interface.flashPlayerId).pauseSong();
















}
catch
(e)
{


















return;
















}












},














getFlashState:
function()
{
















try
{


















return
swfobject.getObjectById(Mp3Interface.flashPlayerId).getState();
















}
catch
(e)
{


















return;
















}












},












isInitialized:
function()
{
















return
this.initialized;












},












backupInit:
function
()
{
















if
(this.initialized)
{




















return;
















}

















try
{




















setTimeout(function()
{
























if
(swfobject
&&
swfobject.getObjectById(Mp3Interface.flashPlayerId)
&&
Mp3Interface.getFlashState())
{




























Mp3Interface.callback("onPlayerInit");
























}
else
{




























Mp3Interface.backupInit();
























}




















},100);
















}
catch
(e)

{




















if
(Mp3Interface.retriedInit)
{
























return
;




















}
else
{
























setTimeout(function
()
{




























Mp3Interface.retriedInit
=
true;




























Mp3Interface.backupInit();
























},
500);




















}
















}












},














callback:
function(event)
{
















switch
(event)
{




















case
'onPlayerInit':
























for
(var
i
in

)
{

=

(obj)

(navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Safari")

{

{

obj;

}

























}

















return
obj;













}

(navigator.appName.indexOf("Microsoft
Internet")==-1)
{

















if
(document.embeds
&&

return

else
{

}








}

function
ep_getAMDCookieValue()
{












var
flashAMDCookieValue
=
null;












var
albumSampler
=
ep_getFlashMovieObject("ep_AMPlayerProd");












if
(albumSampler
==
null)
{
















albumSampler
=
ep_getFlashMovieObject("fe_ep_AMPlayerProd");












}












if
(albumSampler
&&

===
'function')
{














flashAMDCookieValue
=

}
















return
flashAMDCookieValue;








}









function
varIsUndef(v)
{












return
((v
==
undefined)
||
(v
==
null)
||
(v
==
"undefined")
||
(v
==
"null"));








}









var
createBrowserCookie
=
function(domain,
name,
value)
{












var
date
=
new
Date();












date.setTime(date.getTime()+(10*365*24*60*60*1000));













var
expires
=
";
expires="+date.toGMTString();












return
name+"="+value+expires+";
path=/;
domain="
+
domain;








};









function
getAmdPluginValue()
{












var
value
=
null;












if
(window.ActiveXObject)
{
















try
{




















amd
=
new
ActiveXObject("Amazon.AmazonMP3DownloaderPlugin");




















value
=
amd
?
amd.version
:
null;
















}
catch(e)
{}












}
else
if(navigator.plugins)
{
















navigator.plugins.refresh();
















amd
=
navigator.plugins["AmazonMP3DownloaderPlugin"];
















var
regex
=
/.*?([0-9]+[.][0-9]+[.][0-9]+)$/;
















value
=
(amd
&&
amd.description.match(regex))
?
amd.description.match(regex)[1]
:
null;












}












return
value;








}









function
syncFlashAndHTTPCookies()
{












var
cookieSync
=
"normal";












var
flashAMDCookieValue
=
undefined;












if(cookieSync
!=
"install"
&&
cookieSync
!=
"uninstall")
{

















flashAMDCookieValue
=
ep_getAMDCookieValue();












}












var
httpAMDCookieValue;












var
cookieName
=
"dmusic_download_manager_enabled";












var
domain
=
".amazon.com";












if(document.cookie
!=
null)
{
















var
ca
=
document.cookie.split(';');
















for(var
i=0;i
<
ca.length;i++)
{




















var
c
=
ca[i];




















while
(c.charAt(0)=='
')
c
=
c.substring(1,c.length);




















if
(c.indexOf(cookieName)
==
0)
{
























httpAMDCookieValue
=
c.substring(cookieName.length,c.length);
























break;




















}
















}












}












var
vals
=
"flashAMDCookieValue:
"
+
flashAMDCookieValue
+
",
httpAMDCookieValue:
"
+
httpAMDCookieValue
+
",
cookieSync:
"
+
cookieSync;












var
pluginAmdValue
=
getAmdPluginValue();












if(cookieSync
==
"uninstall")
{
















vals
+=
"
action:
uninstall
flashCookie";
















ep_setAMDCookieValue("uninstalled");












}
else
if(cookieSync
==
"install")
{
















vals
+=
"
action:
install
flashCookie";
















ep_setAMDCookieValue(httpAMDCookieValue);












}
else
if
(pluginAmdValue
!=
null)
{














try
{

















document.cookie
=
createBrowserCookie(domain,
cookieName,
pluginAmdValue);
















Mp3Interface.setSharedCookie(cookieName,
pluginAmdValue);
















ep_setAMDCookieValue(pluginAmdValue);
















vals
+=
"
action:
httpCookie
->
flashCookie";














}
catch
(e)
{}












}
else
{

















if(varIsUndef(flashAMDCookieValue)
&&
!varIsUndef(httpAMDCookieValue))
{









































vals
+=
"
action:
httpCookie
->
flashCookie";




















ep_setAMDCookieValue(httpAMDCookieValue);
















}
else
if(flashAMDCookieValue
==
"uninstalled")
{




















vals
+=
"
action:
delete
httpCookie";




















var
expires
=
";
expires=Thu,
01-Jan-1970
00:00:01
GMT";




















document.cookie
=
cookieName+flashAMDCookieValue+expires+";
path=/;
domain="
+
domain;
















}
else
if(!varIsUndef(flashAMDCookieValue)
&&
flashAMDCookieValue
!=
"uninstalled"
&&
varIsUndef(httpAMDCookieValue))
{




















vals
+=
"
action:
httpCookie
<-
flashCookie";




















var
date
=
new
Date();




















date.setTime(date.getTime()+(10*365*24*60*60*1000));




















var
expires
=
";
expires="+date.toGMTString();




















document.cookie
=
cookieName+flashAMDCookieValue+expires+";
path=/;
domain="
+
domain;
















}












}












var
flashHTTPCookieDiv
=
document.getElementById("ep_amdCookie");












if(flashHTTPCookieDiv)
{
















flashHTTPCookieDiv.innerHTML
=
vals;












}








}









if(window.addEventListener)
{














window.addEventListener("load",
syncFlashAndHTTPCookies,
false);








}
else
if(window.attachEvent)
{














window.attachEvent("onload",
syncFlashAndHTTPCookies);








}









if(window.onunload
==
undefined)
{












window.onunload
=
function()
{return
false;};








}

var
ep_so;	





function
ep_loadSwf_Core(swfLocation,
swfWidth,
swfHeight,
flashVersion,
bgColor,
swfParams,
flashParams,
embedAttributes)
{



try
{






ep_so
=
new
SWFObject(swfLocation,
"ep_AMPlayerProd",
swfWidth,
swfHeight,
flashVersion,
bgColor);	










for
(var
v
in
swfParams)
{








ep_so.addVariable(v,
encodeURIComponent(swfParams[v]));






}






for
(var
v
in
flashParams)
{








ep_so.addParam(v,
flashParams[v]);






}






for
(var
v
in
embedAttributes)
{








ep_so.setAttribute(v,
embedAttributes[v]);






}







ep_so.addVariable("swfEmbedTime",
new
Date().getTime());







var
agt
=
navigator.userAgent;














var
reFirefox
=
new
RegExp("firefox/",
"i");






var
regx
=
agt.split(reFirefox);






var
ffVersion
=
8;






if
(regx[1])
{










var
pts
=
regx[1].split(/[.]/);










ffVersion
=
parseFloat(pts[0]
+
"."
+
pts[1]);






}






var
minorVersion
=
parseFloat(navigator.ap);






if
((navigator.appVersion.indexOf("Mac")!=-1)
||
(ffVersion
<
1.5))
{










ep_so.setAttribute("height",
swfHeight);










ep_so.setAttribute("width",
swfWidth);










ep_so.addVariable("oldFirefox",
"1");	











}







if
(ep_so.write("ep_flashcontent"))
{










fp_resizePlayerSpace('ep_',
































450,
































27);






}






else
{










var
nsPrefix
=
'ep_';










fp_resizePlayerSpace(nsPrefix,
0,
0);






}


}
catch(err)
{






fp_resizePlayerSpace('ep_',
0,
0);


}


return
false;
}

<h2
id="artistCentralBio_heading">Biography</h2>









<div
id="artistCentralBio_bios"
class="artistBios">










<p>Low
Country
Blues<br
/>January
18,
2011</p>









<p>&#8220;I&#8217;ve
got
my
hand
over
my
heart,&#8221;
Gregg
Allman
says
of
his
extraordinary
new
album,
&#8220;and
if
it&#8217;s
a
hit
there,
it&#8217;s
a
hit.&#8221;</p>









<p>As
a
founding
member
of
the
one
and
only
Allman
Brothers
Band
and
in
his
own
storied
solo
career,
Allman
has
long
been
a
gifted
natural
interpreter
of
the
blues,
his
soulful
and
distinctive
voice
one
of
the
defining
sounds
in
the
history
of
American
music.
Low
Country
Blues
marks
the
legendary
Rock
...
<a
href="javascript:void(0);"
id="Bio_officialReadMore"
style="display:
inline;">Read
more</a>
</p>








</div>








</div>








<div
id="artistCentralBio_communityFullbios"
class="Bio_ReadMore"
style="">









<div
id="artistCentralBio_FullbiosContent"
class="artistCentralBio_biographyBody">










<p>
</p>









<p>Low
Country
Blues<br
/>January
18,
2011</p>









<p>&#8220;I&#8217;ve
got
my
hand
over
my
heart,&#8221;
Gregg
Allman
says
of
his
extraordinary
new
album,
&#8220;and
if
it&#8217;s
a
hit
there,
it&#8217;s
a
hit.&#8221;</p>









<p>As
a
founding
member
of
the
one
and
only
Allman
Brothers
Band
and
in
his
own
storied
solo
career,
Allman
has
long
been
a
gifted
natural
interpreter
of
the
blues,
his
soulful
and
distinctive
voice
one
of
the
defining
sounds
in
the
history
of
American
music.
Low
Country
Blues
marks
the
legendary
Rock
&amp;
Roll
Hall
of
Famer&#8217;s
seventh
solo
recording
and
first
in
more
than
13
years.
Produced
by
T
Bone
Burnett,
the
album
finds
Allman
putting
his
own
stamp
on
songs
by
some
of
the
blues
giants
whose
work
has
long
influenced
his
own,
from
Muddy
Waters
and
BB
King
to
Buddy
Guy
and
Magic
Sam.
Named
for
the
coastal
Georgia
region
Allman
calls
home,
Low
Country
Blues
stands
as
a
high
water
mark
in
an
already
remarkable
body
of
work,
rich
with
passion,
verve,
and
the
unerring
confidence
of
a
true
survivor.</p>









<p>Though
Allman
has
been
a
constant
presence
on
the
road
over
the
past
decade,
with
The
Allman
Brothers
Band
as
well
as
with
his
own
crack
combo,
he
has
spent
precious
little
time
in
the
studio
since
the
2002
death
of
producer
Tom
Dowd
&#8211;
the
man
behind
the
glass
for
much
of
his
recorded
career.
So
when
his
manager
suggested
he
veer
off
from
a
2009
tour
for
a
Memphis
meeting
with
the
multiple
Grammy
Award-winning
Burnett,
Allman
admits
to
being
not
entirely
enthused.</p>









<p>&#8220;I
said,
&#8216;Oh
man,
I
don&#8217;t
wanna
start
meeting
a
string
of
dudes,
all
of
&#8216;em
trying
to
outdo
the
other
one,&#8221;
he
recalls.
&#8220;But
we
stopped
in
Memphis
and
here
comes
T
Bone.
The
first
sentence
out
of
his
mouth
was
something
like,
&#8216;Tommy
Dowd
was
The
Man,
wasn&#8217;t
he?
I&#8217;ve
patterned
a
lot
of
my
stuff
after
that
gentleman.&#8217;
I
thought,
&#8216;Right,
what&#8217;ve
we
got
here?&#8217;&#8221;</p>









<p>The
two
musicians
quickly
bonded,
chatting
about
favorite
records,
mutual
friends,
and
reminiscences
of
Nashville&#8217;s
renowned
clear
channel
station,
WLAC,
which
introduced
rhythm
&amp;
blues
music
to
a
generation
of
late
night
listeners
from
New
York
to
Miami.</p>









<p>&#8220;He
told
me
some
guy
gave
him
a
hard
drive,
it
has
10,000
obscure
blues
songs,&#8221;
Allman
says.
&#8220;He
says,
&#8216;I&#8217;m
gonna
pick
out
twenty
of
&#8216;em
and
send
&#8216;em
to
ya
and
you
tell
me
what
you
think.&#8217;
He
said,
&#8216;They&#8217;re
old,
like
Billie
Holliday
old,
and
when
you
listen
to
&#8216;em,
I
want
you
to
think
about
us
gettin&#8217;
in
there
and
about
bringin&#8217;
&#8216;em
up
to
today.&#8217;&#8221;</p>









<p>Allman
found
the
idea
irresistible
and
in
January
2010,
a
stunning
combo
was
assembled
at
Los
Angeles&#8217;
The
Village
Recorder,
comprising
Burnett
and
Doyle
Bramhall
II
on
guitars,
backed
by
the
brilliant
rhythm
section
of
upright
bassist
Dennis
Crouch
and
drummer
Jay
Bellerose.
What&#8217;s
more,
the
lineup
included
a
brass
section
arranged
and
conducted
by
trumpeter
Darrell
Leonard,
whose
illustrious
resume
extends
back
to
his
work
with
Delaney
&amp;
Bonnie
&amp;
Friends
(featuring
Gregg&#8217;s
late,
great
brother
Duane).
As
if
that
weren&#8217;t
enough,
sitting
in
on
piano
was
a
dear
old
friend,
the
Night
Tripper
himself,
Mac
&#8220;Dr.
John&#8221;
Rebennack,
with
whom
Allman
co-wrote
&#8220;Let
This
Be
A
Lesson
To
Ya&#8217;&#8221;
on
The
Gregg
Allman
Band&#8217;s
1977
classic,
Playin&#8217;
Up
A
Storm.</p>









<p>&#8220;T
Bone
knew
that
that
him
being
there
would
put
a
certain
fire
in
my
ass,&#8221;
Allman
says.
&#8220;It
was
so
good
seeing
Dr.
John,
both
of
us
being
sober.
&#8216;Cause
last
time
I
saw
him,
both
of
us
were
pretty
much
nose
to
the
floor.
He&#8217;s
such
a
nice
dude,</p>









<p>he&#8217;s
funny,
God,
is
he
funny.
Before
he
was
so
stoned,
it
didn&#8217;t
really
come
out
full
force,
but
oh
man,
he
is
hilarious!&#8221;</p>









<p>This
powerhouse
band
&#8211;
which
of
course
also
features
Gregg&#8217;s
own
acoustic
guitar
expertise
and
trademark
Hammond
B-3
organ
&#8211;
cooks
up
an
earthy
and
atmospheric
musical
stew
infused
with
gritty
R&amp;B
muscle,
spooky
Southern
psychedelia,
and
greasy
deep
soul
grooves.</p>









<p>&#8220;The
band
was
just
a
bitch,
man,&#8221;
Allman
says.
&#8220;It&#8217;s
not
all
just
a
wall
of
guitars
&#8211;
not
that
there&#8217;s
anything
at
all
wrong
with
The
Brothers,
because
that&#8217;s
very,
very
tasty.&#8221;</p>









<p>The
tracking
came
fast
and
furious,
kicking
off
with
an
ominous
take
on
Sleepy
John
Estes&#8217;
ominous
&#8220;Floating
Bridge.&#8221;
From
there,
the
album
covers
the
blues&#8217;
many
emotional
terrains,
from
exuberant
showstoppers
like
Little
Milton&#8217;s
&#8220;Blind
Man&#8221;
and
the
album&#8217;s
one
original
composition,
the
swaggering
&#8220;Just
Another
Rider&#8221;
(co-written
with
longtime
ABB
guitarist
Warren
Haynes),
to
Skip
James&#8217;
haunted
&#8220;Devil
Got
My
Woman&#8221;
and
the
weary
but
unbowed
traditional,
&#8220;Rolling
Stone.&#8221;</p>









<p>&#8220;If
it
works
right,
it
all
turns
real
magic,&#8221;
Allman
says.
&#8220;And
that&#8217;s
what
happened
this
time,
more
so
I
think
than
anything
I&#8217;ve
ever
recorded.
We
got
15
masters
in
11
days;
let
me
tell
ya,
they
just
went
Pop!
Pop!
Pop!
Pop!&#8221;</p>









<p>When
it
came
to
vocals,
Burnett
was
determined
to
push
Allman
out
of
his
comfort
zone,
encouraging
spontaneity
and
soul
above
all
else.
&#8220;First
takes
scare
me
to
death,&#8221;
he
says,
&#8220;they
really
do.
On
about
three
or
maybe
four
of
&#8216;em,
Bone
comes
over
the
microphone,
&#8216;Alright,
we
got
it.&#8217;
I
said,
&#8216;Well
wait,
hold
it,
hold
it!
What
do
you
mean
got
it?
We
just
ran
it
down!&#8217;
&#8216;No,
we
got
it.&#8217;
I
went
back
in
the
control
room,
I
said,
&#8216;Man,
I
know
I
can
get
it
better
than
that.&#8217;
He
says,
&#8216;What&#8217;s
wrong
with
that?&#8217;
I
said,
&#8216;Well,
nothin&#8217;s
wrong
with
it,
I
just
think
I
can
do
it
with
a
little
more
interesting
feel.&#8217;
So
we
went
back
out
there,
I
tried,
man,
I
tried
as
hard
as
I
could.
Nope.&#8221;</p>









<p>Indeed,
Allman&#8217;s
instantly
identifiable
voice
remains
a
wonder,
wringing
nuance
and
history
from
every
lyric.
&#8220;I
have
an
evolved
throat,&#8221;
he
says.
&#8220;I
think
I&#8217;m
a
little
more
meticulous
now.
I&#8217;m
a
real
stickler
for
melody.
I
used
to
think
more
about
beat
than
I
did
about
melody,
but
now
I
think
about
both
of
&#8216;em.
See,
you&#8217;ve
got
to
have
beat,
because
first
of
all,
you&#8217;ve
got
to
feel
something
as
well
as
hear
it.
Both
of
those
entities
have
to
be
really
personified
in
my
book.&#8221;</p>









<p>Like
any
genuine
bluesman,
Allman&#8217;s
own
life
has
been
colored
by
myriad
triumphs
and
too
many
tragedies.
Low
Country
Blues
was
initially
slated
for
a
mid-2010
release,
but
that
plan
changed
when
Gregg,
who
had
long
battled
chronic
Hepatitis
C,
was
notified
that
he
was
a
candidate
for
a
liver
transplant.
In
June
2010,
he
entered
the
Mayo
Clinic
in
Jacksonville,
Florida
where
he
successfully
underwent
the
difficult
surgery.
Knowing
that
he
had
only
just
made
one
of
the
defining
albums
of
his
recorded
career
proved
to
be
the
best
medicine,
giving
Allman
the
inner
strength
he
needed
to
fully
heal.</p>









<p>&#8220;This
record&#8217;s
one
of
the
things
that&#8217;s
held
me
together,&#8221;
he
says.
&#8220;Because
when
I
woke
up
in
the
hospital
from
this
incredibly
big
surgery,
I
held
on
to
the
idea
that,
hey
man,
you&#8217;ve
got
a
record
in
the
can!&#8221;</p>









<p>An
inveterate
road
warrior,
Allman
is
understandably
itching
to
return
to
the
endless
highway.
He
spent
the
months
following
the
surgery
hitting
both
the
gym
and
the
rehearsal
studio,
working
hard
to
restore
his
vitality
to
its
requisite
level.
Moreover,
Allman
is
justifiably
proud
of
Low
Country
Blues
and
is
eager
to
get
out
there
to
bring
these
songs
to
his
countless
fans.</p>









<p>&#8220;When
you
have
a
new
record
it
always
feels
different,&#8221;
he
says.
&#8220;Man,
you
gotta
get
out
there
and
move
the
muscles,
you
gotta
move
it
and
shake
it.&#8221;</p>









<p>&#8220;It&#8217;s
been
too
long,&#8221;
he
adds.
&#8220;I
guess
I
was
just
born
with
a
lot
of
gypsy
in
my
soul.&#8221;</p>









<p>Simply
put,
Low
Country
Blues
is
Gregg
Allman
at
his
very
best,
a
self-assured,
spirited
collection
that
will
stand
as
a
major
milestone
in
what
is
undeniably
an
exceptional
career.
&#8220;Places
you
been,
things
that
you
done/Somehow
you&#8217;re
still
on
the
run,&#8221;
Allman
sings
on
&#8220;Just
Another
Rider.&#8221;
Long
may
he
run.</p>










<p></p>

<div

class="artistCentralBio_biographyBody">










<p>
</p>









<p>Low
Country
Blues<br
/>January
18,
2011</p>









<p>&#8220;I&#8217;ve
got
my
hand
over
my
heart,&#8221;
Gregg
Allman
says
of
his
extraordinary
new
album,
&#8220;and
if
it&#8217;s
a
hit
there,
it&#8217;s
a
hit.&#8221;</p>









<p>As
a
founding
member
of
the
one
and
only
Allman
Brothers
Band
and
in
his
own
storied
solo
career,
Allman
has
long
been
a
gifted
natural
interpreter
of
the
blues,
his
soulful
and
distinctive
voice
one
of
the
defining
sounds
in
the
history
of
American
music.
Low
Country
Blues
marks
the
legendary
Rock
&amp;
Roll
Hall
of
Famer&#8217;s
seventh
solo
recording
and
first
in
more
than
13
years.
Produced
by
T
Bone
Burnett,
the
album
finds
Allman
putting
his
own
stamp
on
songs
by
some
of
the
blues
giants
whose
work
has
long
influenced
his
own,
from
Muddy
Waters
and
BB
King
to
Buddy
Guy
and
Magic
Sam.
Named
for
the
coastal
Georgia
region
Allman
calls
home,
Low
Country
Blues
stands
as
a
high
water
mark
in
an
already
remarkable
body
of
work,
rich
with
passion,
verve,
and
the
unerring
confidence
of
a
true
survivor.</p>









<p>Though
Allman
has
been
a
constant
presence
on
the
road
over
the
past
decade,
with
The
Allman
Brothers
Band
as
well
as
with
his
own
crack
combo,
he
has
spent
precious
little
time
in
the
studio
since
the
2002
death
of
producer
Tom
Dowd
&#8211;
the
man
behind
the
glass
for
much
of
his
recorded
career.
So
when
his
manager
suggested
he
veer
off
from
a
2009
tour
for
a
Memphis
meeting
with
the
multiple
Grammy
Award-winning
Burnett,
Allman
admits
to
being
not
entirely
enthused.</p>









<p>&#8220;I
said,
&#8216;Oh
man,
I
don&#8217;t
wanna
start
meeting
a
string
of
dudes,
all
of
&#8216;em
trying
to
outdo
the
other
one,&#8221;
he
recalls.
&#8220;But
we
stopped
in
Memphis
and
here
comes
T
Bone.
The
first
sentence
out
of
his
mouth
was
something
like,
&#8216;Tommy
Dowd
was
The
Man,
wasn&#8217;t
he?
I&#8217;ve
patterned
a
lot
of
my
stuff
after
that
gentleman.&#8217;
I
thought,
&#8216;Right,
what&#8217;ve
we
got
here?&#8217;&#8221;</p>









<p>The
two
musicians
quickly
bonded,
chatting
about
favorite
records,
mutual
friends,
and
reminiscences
of
Nashville&#8217;s
renowned
clear
channel
station,
WLAC,
which
introduced
rhythm
&amp;
blues
music
to
a
generation
of
late
night
listeners
from
New
York
to
Miami.</p>









<p>&#8220;He
told
me
some
guy
gave
him
a
hard
drive,
it
has
10,000
obscure
blues
songs,&#8221;
Allman
says.
&#8220;He
says,
&#8216;I&#8217;m
gonna
pick
out
twenty
of
&#8216;em
and
send
&#8216;em
to
ya
and
you
tell
me
what
you
think.&#8217;
He
said,
&#8216;They&#8217;re
old,
like
Billie
Holliday
old,
and
when
you
listen
to
&#8216;em,
I
want
you
to
think
about
us
gettin&#8217;
in
there
and
about
bringin&#8217;
&#8216;em
up
to
today.&#8217;&#8221;</p>









<p>Allman
found
the
idea
irresistible
and
in
January
2010,
a
stunning
combo
was
assembled
at
Los
Angeles&#8217;
The
Village
Recorder,
comprising
Burnett
and
Doyle
Bramhall
II
on
guitars,
backed
by
the
brilliant
rhythm
section
of
upright
bassist
Dennis
Crouch
and
drummer
Jay
Bellerose.
What&#8217;s
more,
the
lineup
included
a
brass
section
arranged
and
conducted
by
trumpeter
Darrell
Leonard,
whose
illustrious
resume
extends
back
to
his
work
with
Delaney
&amp;
Bonnie
&amp;
Friends
(featuring
Gregg&#8217;s
late,
great
brother
Duane).
As
if
that
weren&#8217;t
enough,
sitting
in
on
piano
was
a
dear
old
friend,
the
Night
Tripper
himself,
Mac
&#8220;Dr.
John&#8221;
Rebennack,
with
whom
Allman
co-wrote
&#8220;Let
This
Be
A
Lesson
To
Ya&#8217;&#8221;
on
The
Gregg
Allman
Band&#8217;s
1977
classic,
Playin&#8217;
Up
A
Storm.</p>









<p>&#8220;T
Bone
knew
that
that
him
being
there
would
put
a
certain
fire
in
my
ass,&#8221;
Allman
says.
&#8220;It
was
so
good
seeing
Dr.
John,
both
of
us
being
sober.
&#8216;Cause
last
time
I
saw
him,
both
of
us
were
pretty
much
nose
to
the
floor.
He&#8217;s
such
a
nice
dude,</p>









<p>he&#8217;s
funny,
God,
is
he
funny.
Before
he
was
so
stoned,
it
didn&#8217;t
really
come
out
full
force,
but
oh
man,
he
is
hilarious!&#8221;</p>









<p>This
powerhouse
band
&#8211;
which
of
course
also
features
Gregg&#8217;s
own
acoustic
guitar
expertise
and
trademark
Hammond
B-3
organ
&#8211;
cooks
up
an
earthy
and
atmospheric
musical
stew
infused
with
gritty
R&amp;B
muscle,
spooky
Southern
psychedelia,
and
greasy
deep
soul
grooves.</p>









<p>&#8220;The
band
was
just
a
bitch,
man,&#8221;
Allman
says.
&#8220;It&#8217;s
not
all
just
a
wall
of
guitars
&#8211;
not
that
there&#8217;s
anything
at
all
wrong
with
The
Brothers,
because
that&#8217;s
very,
very
tasty.&#8221;</p>









<p>The
tracking
came
fast
and
furious,
kicking
off
with
an
ominous
take
on
Sleepy
John
Estes&#8217;
ominous
&#8220;Floating
Bridge.&#8221;
From
there,
the
album
covers
the
blues&#8217;
many
emotional
terrains,
from
exuberant
showstoppers
like
Little
Milton&#8217;s
&#8220;Blind
Man&#8221;
and
the
album&#8217;s
one
original
composition,
the
swaggering
&#8220;Just
Another
Rider&#8221;
(co-written
with
longtime
ABB
guitarist
Warren
Haynes),
to
Skip
James&#8217;
haunted
&#8220;Devil
Got
My
Woman&#8221;
and
the
weary
but
unbowed
traditional,
&#8220;Rolling
Stone.&#8221;</p>









<p>&#8220;If
it
works
right,
it
all
turns
real
magic,&#8221;
Allman
says.
&#8220;And
that&#8217;s
what
happened
this
time,
more
so
I
think
than
anything
I&#8217;ve
ever
recorded.
We
got
15
masters
in
11
days;
let
me
tell
ya,
they
just
went
Pop!
Pop!
Pop!
Pop!&#8221;</p>









<p>When
it
came
to
vocals,
Burnett
was
determined
to
push
Allman
out
of
his
comfort
zone,
encouraging
spontaneity
and
soul
above
all
else.
&#8220;First
takes
scare
me
to
death,&#8221;
he
says,
&#8220;they
really
do.
On
about
three
or
maybe
four
of
&#8216;em,
Bone
comes
over
the
microphone,
&#8216;Alright,
we
got
it.&#8217;
I
said,
&#8216;Well
wait,
hold
it,
hold
it!
What
do
you
mean
got
it?
We
just
ran
it
down!&#8217;
&#8216;No,
we
got
it.&#8217;
I
went
back
in
the
control
room,
I
said,
&#8216;Man,
I
know
I
can
get
it
better
than
that.&#8217;
He
says,
&#8216;What&#8217;s
wrong
with
that?&#8217;
I
said,
&#8216;Well,
nothin&#8217;s
wrong
with
it,
I
just
think
I
can
do
it
with
a
little
more
interesting
feel.&#8217;
So
we
went
back
out
there,
I
tried,
man,
I
tried
as
hard
as
I
could.
Nope.&#8221;</p>









<p>Indeed,
Allman&#8217;s
instantly
identifiable
voice
remains
a
wonder,
wringing
nuance
and
history
from
every
lyric.
&#8220;I
have
an
evolved
throat,&#8221;
he
says.
&#8220;I
think
I&#8217;m
a
little
more
meticulous
now.
I&#8217;m
a
real
stickler
for
melody.
I
used
to
think
more
about
beat
than
I
did
about
melody,
but
now
I
think
about
both
of
&#8216;em.
See,
you&#8217;ve
got
to
have
beat,
because
first
of
all,
you&#8217;ve
got
to
feel
something
as
well
as
hear
it.
Both
of
those
entities
have
to
be
really
personified
in
my
book.&#8221;</p>









<p>Like
any
genuine
bluesman,
Allman&#8217;s
own
life
has
been
colored
by
myriad
triumphs
and
too
many
tragedies.
Low
Country
Blues
was
initially
slated
for
a
mid-2010
release,
but
that
plan
changed
when
Gregg,
who
had
long
battled
chronic
Hepatitis
C,
was
notified
that
he
was
a
candidate
for
a
liver
transplant.
In
June
2010,
he
entered
the
Mayo
Clinic
in
Jacksonville,
Florida
where
he
successfully
underwent
the
difficult
surgery.
Knowing
that
he
had
only
just
made
one
of
the
defining
albums
of
his
recorded
career
proved
to
be
the
best
medicine,
giving
Allman
the
inner
strength
he
needed
to
fully
heal.</p>









<p>&#8220;This
record&#8217;s
one
of
the
things
that&#8217;s
held
me
together,&#8221;
he
says.
&#8220;Because
when
I
woke
up
in
the
hospital
from
this
incredibly
big
surgery,
I
held
on
to
the
idea
that,
hey
man,
you&#8217;ve
got
a
record
in
the
can!&#8221;</p>









<p>An
inveterate
road
warrior,
Allman
is
understandably
itching
to
return
to
the
endless
highway.
He
spent
the
months
following
the
surgery
hitting
both
the
gym
and
the
rehearsal
studio,
working
hard
to
restore
his
vitality
to
its
requisite
level.
Moreover,
Allman
is
justifiably
proud
of
Low
Country
Blues
and
is
eager
to
get
out
there
to
bring
these
songs
to
his
countless
fans.</p>









<p>&#8220;When
you
have
a
new
record
it
always
feels
different,&#8221;
he
says.
&#8220;Man,
you
gotta
get
out
there
and
move
the
muscles,
you
gotta
move
it
and
shake
it.&#8221;</p>









<p>&#8220;It&#8217;s
been
too
long,&#8221;
he
adds.
&#8220;I
guess
I
was
just
born
with
a
lot
of
gypsy
in
my
soul.&#8221;</p>









<p>Simply
put,
Low
Country
Blues
is
Gregg
Allman
at
his
very
best,
a
self-assured,
spirited
collection
that
will
stand
as
a
major
milestone
in
what
is
undeniably
an
exceptional
career.
&#8220;Places
you
been,
things
that
you
done/Somehow
you&#8217;re
still
on
the
run,&#8221;
Allman
sings
on
&#8220;Just
Another
Rider.&#8221;
Long
may
he
run.</p>

<p>Low
Country
Blues<br
/>January
18,
2011</p>









<p>&#8220;I&#8217;ve
got
my
hand
over
my
heart,&#8221;
Gregg
Allman
says
of
his
extraordinary
new
album,
&#8220;and
if
it&#8217;s
a
hit
there,
it&#8217;s
a
hit.&#8221;</p>









<p>As
a

member
of
the

only
Allman

in
his

earthy
and
atmospheric
musical
stew
infused
with
gritty
R&amp;B
muscle,
spooky
Southern
psychedelia,
and
greasy
deep
soul
grooves.</p>









<p>&#8220;The
band
was
just
a
bitch,
man,&#8221;
Allman
says.
&#8220;It&#8217;s
not
all
just
a
wall
of
guitars
&#8211;
not
that
there&#8217;s
anything
at
all
wrong
with
The
Brothers,
because
that&#8217;s
very,
very
tasty.&#8221;</p>









<p>The
tracking
came
fast
and
furious,
kicking
off
with
an
ominous
take
on
Sleepy
John
Estes&#8217;
ominous
&#8220;Floating
Bridge.&#8221;
From
there,
the
album
covers
the
blues&#8217;
many
emotional
terrains,
from
exuberant
showstoppers
like
Little
Milton&#8217;s
&#8220;Blind
Man&#8221;
and
the
album&#8217;s
one
original
composition,
the
swaggering
&#8220;Just
Another
Rider&#8221;
(co-written
with
longtime
ABB
guitarist
Warren
Haynes),
to
Skip
James&#8217;
haunted
&#8220;Devil
Got
My
Woman&#8221;
and
the
weary
but
unbowed
traditional,
&#8220;Rolling
Stone.&#8221;</p>









<p>&#8220;If
it
works
right,
it
all
turns
real
magic,&#8221;
Allman
says.
&#8220;And
that&#8217;s
what
happened
this
time,
more
so
I
think
than
anything
I&#8217;ve
ever
recorded.
We
got
15
masters
in
11
days;
let
me
tell
ya,
they
just
went
Pop!
Pop!
Pop!
Pop!&#8221;</p>









<p>When
it
came
to
vocals,
Burnett
was
determined
to
push
Allman
out
of
his
comfort
zone,
encouraging
spontaneity
and
soul
above
all
else.
&#8220;First
takes
scare
me
to
death,&#8221;
he
says,
&#8220;they
really
do.
On
about
three
or
maybe
four
of
&#8216;em,
Bone
comes
over
the
microphone,
&#8216;Alright,
we
got
it.&#8217;
I
said,
&#8216;Well
wait,
hold
it,
hold
it!
What
do
you
mean
got
it?
We
just
ran
it
down!&#8217;
&#8216;No,
we
got
it.&#8217;
I
went
back
in
the
control
room,
I
said,
&#8216;Man,
I
know
I
can
get
it
better
than
that.&#8217;
He
says,
&#8216;What&#8217;s
wrong
with
that?&#8217;
I
said,
&#8216;Well,
nothin&#8217;s
wrong
with
it,
I
just
think
I
can
do
it
with
a
little
more
interesting
feel.&#8217;
So
we
went
back
out
there,
I
tried,
man,
I
tried
as
hard
as
I
could.
Nope.&#8221;</p>









<p>Indeed,
Allman&#8217;s
instantly
identifiable
voice
remains
a
wonder,
wringing
nuance
and
history
from
every
lyric.
&#8220;I
have
an
evolved
throat,&#8221;
he
says.
&#8220;I
think
I&#8217;m
a
little
more
meticulous
now.
I&#8217;m
a
real
stickler
for
melody.
I
used
to
think
more
about
beat
than
I
did
about
melody,
but
now
I
think
about
both
of
&#8216;em.
See,
you&#8217;ve
got
to
have
beat,
because
first
of
all,
you&#8217;ve
got
to
feel
something
as
well
as
hear
it.
Both
of
those
entities
have
to
be
really
personified
in
my
book.&#8221;</p>









<p>Like
any
genuine
bluesman,
Allman&#8217;s
own
life
has
been
colored
by
myriad
triumphs
and
too
many
tragedies.
Low
Country
Blues
was
initially
slated
for
a
mid-2010
release,
but
that
plan
changed
when
Gregg,
who
had
long
battled
chronic
Hepatitis
C,
was
notified
that
he
was
a
candidate
for
a
liver
transplant.
In
June
2010,
he
entered
the
Mayo
Clinic
in
Jacksonville,
Florida
where
he
successfully
underwent
the
difficult
surgery.
Knowing
that
he
had
only
just
made
one
of
the
defining
albums
of
his
recorded
career
proved
to
be
the
best
medicine,
giving
Allman
the
inner
strength
he
needed
to
fully
heal.</p>









<p>&#8220;This
record&#8217;s
one
of
the
things
that&#8217;s
held
me
together,&#8221;
he
says.
&#8220;Because
when
I
woke
up
in
the
hospital
from
this
incredibly
big
surgery,
I
held
on
to
the
idea
that,
hey
man,
you&#8217;ve
got
a
record
in
the
can!&#8221;</p>









<p>An
inveterate
road
warrior,
Allman
is
understandably
itching
to
return
to
the
endless
highway.
He
spent
the
months
following
the
surgery
hitting
both
the
gym
and
the
rehearsal
studio,
working
hard
to
restore
his
vitality
to
its
requisite
level.
Moreover,
Allman
is
justifiably
proud
of
Low
Country
Blues
and
is
eager
to
get
out
there
to
bring
these
songs
to
his
countless
fans.</p>









<p>&#8220;When
you
have
a
new
record
it
always
feels
different,&#8221;
he
says.
&#8220;Man,
you
gotta
get
out
there
and
move
the
muscles,
you
gotta
move
it
and
shake
it.&#8221;</p>









<p>&#8220;It&#8217;s
been
too
long,&#8221;
he
adds.
&#8220;I
guess
I
was
just
born
with
a
lot
of
gypsy
in
my
soul.&#8221;</p>









<p>Simply
put,
Low
Country
Blues
is
Gregg
Allman
at
his
very
best,
a
self-assured,
spirited
collection
that
will
stand
as
a
major
milestone
in
what
is
undeniably
an
exceptional
career.
&#8220;Places
you
been,
things
that
you
done/Somehow
you&#8217;re
still
on
the
run,&#8221;
Allman
sings
on
&#8220;Just
Another
Rider.&#8221;
Long
may
he
run.</p>










<p></p>

function
artistCentralBio_toggle(
parentElementId,
activeElementId,
activeClassName,
inactiveClassName
)
{




var
elements
=
jQuery(
'#'
+
parentElementId
).children();




for
(
var
idx
in
elements
)
{








var
element
=
elements[idx];








if(element.id
!='Separator')
{










element.className
=
(
element.id
==
activeElementId
)
?
activeClassName
:
inactiveClassName;








}




}
}

function
artistCentralBio_showBio(
bioName
)
{




var
showBioId
=
'artistCentralBio_'
+
bioName
+
'Bio';




var
showTabId
=
showBioId
+
'Tab';




if
(
jQuery(
'#'
+
showTabId
).className
!=
'artistCentralBio_currentTab'
)
{








artistCentralBio_toggle(
'artistCentralBio_tabsUl',
showTabId,
'artistCentralBio_currentTab',
'artistCentralBio_notCurrentTab'
);








artistCentralBio_toggle(
'artistCentralBio_bios',
showBioId,
'artistCentralBio_activeBio',
'artistCentralBio_inactiveBio'
);




}
}

function
artistCentralBio_printBio(
bioElementId,
modalHeaderText
)
{




var
width

=
680;




var
height
=

left


=
(screen.width
-

/
2;




var
top



=

-

/
2;




var
temp


=

'',

+
',height='
+
height
+
',top='
+

+
',left='
+

);





temp.document.open(
'text/html'
);




temp.document.write(
'<html>'
);




temp.document.write(
'<head><title>'
+
modalHeaderText
+
'</title></head>'
);




//
DON'T

-

gets

to

);

);

);

-

)

)

);

}

/*

*/

=
function(t){

=

:

/*


Success
handler
for

*/
successRemoveFunction
=
function(data,textStatus)
{

=

=

}

/*

Error
handler
for
removal
*/

=
function(tag,asin,t){


if(tgSearch.lastChance[asin]){

=

+
asin);

+
'</div>'
+
displayUndoButton(t));




tgSearch.lastChance[asin]
=
undefined;


}else{




tgSearch.lastChance[asin]
=
1;




submitRemoveTag(t);


}
}


/*

');return

return

}

for

an

*/

function(t){

{

function()
{

},




success
:

cache
:
false,




timeout
:
tgSearch.TIMEOUT,




dataType:
"json",




type:
"POST",




async:
true


};


jQuery.ajax(options);
}

/*

Success
handler
for
adding
a
tag
*/
successAddFunction
=
function(data,textStatus)
{


thisTaggedItem
=
getTaggedItemByASIN(data['asin']);


thisTaggedItem.status
=
data['status'];


thisTaggedItem.enabled
=
data['enabled'];


tgSearch.numberTagged
=
data['numberTagged'];


addTagResults(thisTaggedItem,
data['tagCountString']);
}

/*

Error
handler
for
adding
a
tag
*/
errorAddFunction
=
function(asin,t){


if(tgSearch.lastChance[asin]){




t.status
=
'adderr';




updateTaggedItem(t);




tgSearch.lastChance[asin]
=
undefined;


}else{




tgSearch.lastChance[asin]
=
1;




submitAddTag(t);


}
}


/*

Display
a
search
result,
with
the
correct
action
button
*/
displaySearchResult
=
function(a,
status){


var
t
=
null;
































































































































































if(tgSearch.taggedItemsByASIN[a.asin]
!=
null){




t
=
tgSearch.taggedItemsByASIN[a.asin];


}
































































































































































if(tgSearch.itemAlreadyTagged[a.asin]){




if(t
!=
null){






t.action
=
'ptagged';




}


}
































































































































































var
button;


if(tgSearch.itemAlreadyTagged[a.asin]){




button
=
'<span
class="tgSearchAlreadyTagged">'
+
tgSearch.strings.alreadyTagged
+'</span>';


}else
if(status
==
'waiting'){




button
=
displayWaitingIcon();


}else
if(t
!=
null
&&
t.action
!=
'removed'){




button
=
'<span
class="tgSearchTagged">'
+
tgSearch.strings.taggedMessage
+
'</span>';


}else{




button
=
displayAddTagButton(a);


}
































































































































































var
searchResultDisplay
=
'<td
id="searchItemButton'
+
a.asin
+
'"
class="tiny"
style="color:
#9d0000;
padding:
4px;"
align="center">'
+




button
+




'</td>'
+




displayASIN(a,
'tiny');


return
searchResultDisplay;
}

again
*/
displayNullSearchResults
=
function(){


jQuery("#tgSearchDiv").scrollTop
=
0;
































































































































































var
searchResultsDisplay
=
tgSearch.strings.searchNoResultsMessage;


if(tgSearch.alternateKeywords.length
>
0){




searchResultsDisplay
+=
displayAlternateKeywords();


}


jQuery("#tgSearchDiv").html(searchResultsDisplay);


jQuery("#tgSearchNavigationDiv").html('');
}

/*

ASIN
row
in

results
*/
displayASIN
=
function(a,fontClass,translucent){

==
null){




fontClass
=
'small';


}


if(translucent
==
undefined){




translucent
=
0;


}
































































































































































//display
an
ASIN


var
linkedTitle
=
'<a
class="tgSearchItemTitle"
href="'
+
a.url
+
'">'
+
a.title
+
'</a>';


var
thumbDisplay;


if(a.thumb
!=
null){




thumbDisplay
=
a.thumb;


}else{




thumbDisplay
=
'&nbsp;';


}
































































































































































var
bylineDisplay
=
'';


if(a.byline
!=
''){




bylineDisplay
=
tgSearch.strings.byLine
+
'
'
+
a.byline;


}
































































































































































var
bindingDisplay
=
'';


if(a.binding
!=
''){




bindingDisplay

<span
class="tgSearchBinding">('
+
a.binding
+

}

asinDisplay

;


if(translucent){




asinDisplay
+=
'
tgSearchTranslucent';

asinDisplay
+=
'"
style="padding:
4px;">'
+




linkedTitle
+




'<br
/>'
+




bylineDisplay
+




bindingDisplay
+




'</td>';


return
asinDisplay;
}


/*

==

=

class="tgSearchAlternate">'
+
tgSearch.strings.alternateMessage;

i<tgSearch.alternateKeywords.length;
i++){




keyword
=
tgSearch.alternateKeywords[i];




alternateString
+=

<a
href="javascript:void(0)"
onclick="doAlternateSearch('
+








String.fromCharCode(0x27)
+
keyword
+
String.fromCharCode(0x27)
+








');return
false;">'
+
keyword
+
'</a>';


}
































































































































































alternateString
+=
tgSearch.strings.alternateEndMessage
+
'</div>';

}

/*

=

=

+

+

+

+

}

/*

Update
the
given
tagged
item,
refreshing
its
status
*/
updateTaggedItem
=
function(item){


if(typeof
item
==
'undefined'
||
typeof
item.jqObj
==
'undefined'){




return;


}


item.jqObj.html(displayTaggedItem(item));
}

/*

Remove
the
given
tagged
item
from
the
tagged
items
panel
*/
removeTaggedItem
=
function(item){


if(typeof
item
==
'undefined'
||
typeof
item.jqObj
==
'undefined'){




return;


}


if(item.jqObj.next().attr('class')
==
'tiDivider'){




item.jqObj.next().remove();


}


item.jqObj.remove();
}

displayDivider
=
function(){


return
'<tr
class="tiDivider"><td
colspan="4"
style="border-top:
1px
solid
#eee;">'
+
tgSearch.images.pixel
+
'</td></tr>';
}

function(){

=
'<td
align="center"
id="tgSearchNextTeaserButton">'
+




'<a
href="#"
onClick="displaySearchResults('
+




(tgSearch.currentPage
+
1)
+




',1);return
false;">'

tgSearch.images.next
+

+




'</td>'
+




'<td
colspan="2"
id="tgSearchNextTeaserText">'
+




'<span
class="tgSearchNextTeaser">'
+
tgSearch.strings.nextTeaserMessage
+'</span>'
+




'</td>';


return

}

/*

Show
a
loading
icon,
given
a
location
to

in.
*/
showLoading
=
function(location){


if(location
!=
null){




var
msg
=
tgSearch.strings.loadingMessage;




location.html(msg
+
'
'
+
tgSearch.images.loading);


}
}

/*

Renders
and
displays
search
results
to
the
user
*/
displaySearchResults
=
function(page,
reset){


tgSearch.currentPage
=
page;


//reset
the
search
div's
scroll
for
IE's
sake


if(reset){




jQuery("#tgSearchDiv").scrollTop
=
0;


}


if(tgSearch.resultsLoaded
-
(page
*
tgSearch.searchPageSize)
<=
50
&&
tgSearch.lastElement
==
-1){




startSearch(0);


}
































































































































































if((page
*
tgSearch.searchPageSize)
>
tgSearch.resultsLoaded
&&
tgSearch.lastElement
==
-1){




var
msg
=
tgSearch.strings.loadingMessage;




jQuery("#tgSearchDiv").html(msg
+
'
'
+
tgSearch.images.loading);




return;


}


jQuery("#tgSearchTitle").html(tgSearch.title);


var
pageStart
=
(page
-
1)
*
tgSearch.searchPageSize;


var
pageEnd
=
(page
*
tgSearch.searchPageSize)
-
1;
































































































































































//iterate
through
results
and
call
displaySearchResult


var
resultsShown
=
0;


var
searchResultsDisplay
=
'<table
border="0"
cellpadding="0"
cellspacing="0">';


for(var
i=pageStart;
i<pageEnd;
i++){




if(tgSearch.searchResults[i]
==
null){






break;




}




if(tgSearch.searchResults[i].ASIN.asin
!=
null){






var
item
=
tgSearch.searchResultsByASIN[tgSearch.searchResults[i].ASIN.asin];






if(item.status
!=
'show'){








continue;






}






resultsShown++;






searchResultsDisplay
+=
'<tr
id="tgSearchItem_'
+
tgSearch.searchResults[i].ASIN.asin
+
'">'
+








displaySearchResult(tgSearch.searchResults[i].ASIN,
tgSearch.searchResults[i].status)
+








'</tr>';




}


}


if(!resultsShown
&&
(tgSearch.lastElement
==
-1

||
tgSearch.lastElement
>=
(tgSearch.searchPageSize
*
tgSearch.currentPage))){




searchResultsDisplay
+=
'<tr>'
+




displayNextTeaser()
+




'</tr>';


}


searchResultsDisplay
+=
'</table>';






jQuery("#tgSearchDiv").html(searchResultsDisplay);


displaySearchNavigation();
}

/*

This
function
decides
whether
there
is
a
next
page
to
show,
and
if
we
can
go

to
a
previous
page,
and
renders
buttons
below
the
search
pane
to
let
the
user

perform
the
available
actions
*/
displaySearchNavigation
=
function(){


var
searchNavigationDisplay;


if(tgSearch.currentPage
>=
1){




var
hasNextPage;
//
If
there
is
no
last
element
defined
yet,
or
we're
not
on
the
last
page,
we
can
go
further




if(tgSearch.lastElement
==
-1
||
tgSearch.lastElement
>=
(tgSearch.searchPageSize*tgSearch.currentPage)){






hasNextPage
=
1;




}else{






hasNextPage
=
0;






tgSearch.lastPage
=
tgSearch.currentPage;




}


































































































































































var
itemInfoText;




itemInfoText
=
'<b
class="tiny">'
+
tgSearch.strings.infoMessage
+
'
'
+
tgSearch.currentPage;




if(tgSearch.lastPage
!=
-1){







itemInfoText
+=
'
of
'
+
tgSearch.lastPage;




}




itemInfoText
+=
'</b>';


































































































































































searchNavigationDisplay
=






'<table
class="tgSearchNavTable"
border="0"
cellpadding="0"
cellspacing="0">'
+






'<tr><td
width="50%">&nbsp;</td>';


































































































































































if(tgSearch.currentPage
>
1){






searchNavigationDisplay
+=
'<td
align="right">'
+








'<a
href="#"
onClick="displaySearchResults('
+








(tgSearch.currentPage
-
1)
+








',
1);return
false;"
title="'
+
tgSearch.strings.previousMessage
+
'">'
+
tgSearch.images.previous
+
'</a>'
+








'</td>';




}


































































































































































if(itemInfoText
!=
null){






searchNavigationDisplay
+=
'<td
align="center"
class="tgSearchNavInfo">'
+








itemInfoText
+








'</td>';




}




if(hasNextPage){





searchNavigationDisplay
+=
'<td
align="left">'
+







'<a
href="#"
onClick="displaySearchResults('
+







(tgSearch.currentPage
+
1)
+







',1);return
false;"
title="'
+
tgSearch.strings.nextMessage
+
'">'
+
tgSearch.images.next
+
'</a>'
+







'</td>';




}


































































































































































searchNavigationDisplay
+=
'<td
width="50%">&nbsp;</td></tr>'
+






'</table>';


}else{




searchNavigationDisplay
=
'';


}


if(searchNavigationDisplay
!=
null){




jQuery("#tgSearchNavigationDiv").html(searchNavigationDisplay);


}
}

/*

If
the
search
fails
more
than
once,
display
an
error
*/
showSearchError
=
function(){


jQuery("#tgSearchDiv").html(tgSearch.strings.searchError);
}

/*

Constructor
for
an
ASIN,
given
the
thumbnail
image,
title,
url,
byline,
binding,
and
image
URL.
*/
ASIN
=
function(jsonData)
{


this.asin
=
jsonData['asin'];


this.thumb
=
jsonData['image'];


this.title
=
jsonData['title'];


this.url
=
jsonData['url'];


this.byline
=
jsonData['byline'];


this.binding
=
jsonData['binding'];


this.imageURL
=
jsonData['imageURL'];



jQuery.preloadImage(this.imageURL);
































































































































































//add
a
reference
to
this
object
to
make
it
discoverable


tgSearch.asins[this.asin]
=
this;
}

/*

Construct
a
TaggedItem,
giving
it
an
asin,
an
action
(tagged/undone/previously
tagged),
a
current
status,

and
a
search
number
*/
TaggedItem
=
function(a,action,status,searchNumber){


this.ASIN
=
a;


this.action
=
action;


this.status
=
status;


this.searchNumber
=
searchNumber;
































































































































































tgSearch.taggedItemsByASIN[a.asin]
=
this;
}






























































































































































/*

Construct
a
SearchResult,
given
an
ASIN,
an
action,
and
the
current
status.
*/
SearchResult
=
function(a,action,status){


this.ASIN
=
a;


this.action
=
action;


this.status
=
status;
































































































































































tgSearch.searchResultsByASIN[a.asin]
=
this;
}






























































































































































/*

Retrieve
a
tagged
item
using
its
ASIN
*/
getTaggedItemByASIN
=
function(asin){


var
t
=
tgSearch.taggedItemsByASIN[asin];


return
t;
}

/*

Kick
off
an
asynchronous
search,
using
the
value
in
the
search
box.

If
this
is
not
a
brand-new
search,
then
just
fetch
more
results
for
the
current
search
term.
*/
startSearch
=
function(newSearch){


var
pageNumber
=
1;


if(newSearch){




var
alias
=
jQuery("#tgSearchAlias").attr('value');




var
sValue
=
jQuery("#tgSearchValue").attr('value');




if(sValue.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'')
==
''){






return;




}




if(alias
==
tgSearch.searchAlias
&&
sValue
==
tgSearch.searchValue){






showSearchResults();






return;




}




tgSearch.searchAlias
=
alias;




tgSearch.searchValue
=
sValue.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'');




tgSearch.currentPage
=
1;




tgSearch.currentSearch++;




tgSearch.searchResults
=
new
Array();




tgSearch.searchResultsByASIN
=
new
Object();




tgSearch.resultsLoaded
=
0;




tgSearch.resultsPage
=
1;




tgSearch.searchAliasName
=
jQuery("#tgSearchAlias
option:selected").text();




tgSearch.lastElement
=
-1;




tgSearch.lastPage
=
-1;




tgSearch.alternateKeywords
=
new
Array();




jQuery("#tgSearchTitle").html('');




jQuery("#tgSearchNavigationDiv").html('');


}
else
{




pageNumber
=
tgSearch.resultsPage
-
1;


}
































































































































































//assemble
the
search
URL


var
options
=
{




url
:
"/gp/tagging/addproducts/search.html/ref="
+
tgSearch.ref
+
"_src",




data:
{value
:
tgSearch.searchValue,
page
:
pageNumber,
pageSize
:
tgSearch.resultsPageSize,
index
:
tgSearch.searchAlias,






alias
:
tgSearch.searchAliasName,
queryNo
:
tgSearch.currentSearch,
source
:
tgSearch.source},




error
:
searchErrorHandler,




success
:
searchSuccessFunction,




cache
:
false,




timeout
:
tgSearch.TIMEOUT,




dataType:
"json",




type:
"POST",




async:
true


};





if
(newSearch)
{




tgSearch.resultsPage++;


































































































































































showSearchResults();


































































































































































showLoading(newSearch?jQuery('#tgSearchDiv'):null);


}


jQuery.ajax(options);
}

searchSuccessFunction
=
function(data,textStatus)
{


if
(data['queryNo']
==
tgSearch.currentSearch)
{






tgSearchData
=
new
Object;




if
(data['nextPage'])
{






tgSearchData.nextPage
=
data['nextPage'];




}




if
(data['prevPage'])
{






tgSearchData.prevPage
=
data['prevPage'];




}




tgSearchData.startingItem
=
data['startingItem'];




tgSearchData.endingItem
=
data['endingItem'];




tgSearchData.itemsReturned
=
data['asinList'].length;




tgSearchData.itemsFound
=
data['itemsFound']




tgSearchData.title
=
data['resultsTitle'];




if
(data['correctedKeywords'])
{






tgSearchData.title
+=
'<div
class="tgSearchCorrected">'
+
data['correctedKeywords']
+
'</div>';




}




if
(data['lastItem'])
{






tgSearch.lastElement
=
data['lastItem'];




}




tgSearch.alternateKeywords
=
data['keywordList'];




searchResults(data['asinList'],tgSearchData);


}
}

/*

If
the
search
fails,
try
again
*/
searchErrorHandler
=
function(){


startSearch(0);
}

/*

Success
handler
for
retrieving
search
results
*/
searchResults
=
function(results,searchData){


var
title
=
searchData.title;
































































































































































tgSearch.resultsLoaded
+=
searchData.itemsReturned;
































































































































































for(i=0;
i<results.length;
i++){




var
tmpASIN
=
new
ASIN(results[i]);




if(tmpASIN.asin
!=
null){






tgSearch.searchResults.push(new
SearchResult(tmpASIN,
'add',tgSearch.itemAlreadyTagged[tmpASIN.asin]?'ptagged':'show'));




}


}






























































































































































//
If
we
got
results,
check
to
see
if
there
might
be
alternate
searches.


if(
searchData.itemsReturned
>
0){




if(tgSearch.alternateKeywords.length
>
0){






title
+=
displayAlternateKeywords();




}




tgSearch.title
=
title;




displaySearchResults(tgSearch.currentPage);


}else{
//
If
we
didn't
get
results,
try
to
show
search
suggestions
-
if
there
aren't
any,
display
no
results




if(tgSearch.resultsLoaded
>
0){






tgSearch.lastElement
=
tgSearch.resultsLoaded;






if(tgSearch.alternateKeywords.length
>
0){








title
+=
displayAlternateKeywords();






}






tgSearch.title
=
title;






displaySearchResults(tgSearch.currentPage);




}else{






displayNullSearchResults();




}


}
}

/*

Called
on
1-click
re-search
from
alternate
keywords.

Simply
resets
the
contents
of
the
search

box
to
the
new
search
term
and
performs
a
new
search.
*/
doAlternateSearch
=
function(keyword){


jQuery("#tgSearchValue").attr("value",keyword);


startSearch(1);
}

/*

Make
an
asynchronous
call
to
tag
the
desired
asin.

The
button
clicked
must
be

passed
in
so
we
can
change
it
to
a
waiting
icon.

This
function
just
sets
up

the
waiting
and
item
statuses,
and
calls
a
helper
to
make
the
actual
call.
*/
addTag
=
function(button,asin){


//Find
the
ASIN

a
=
tgSearch.asins[asin];

s
=
tgSearch.searchResultsByASIN[asin];

s.status
=
'tagged';

displaySearchResults(tgSearch.currentPage,0);
































































































































































if(getTaggedItemByASIN(asin)
!=
null){




t
=
getTaggedItemByASIN(asin);




t.action
=
'add';




t.status
=
'waiting';


}else{




t
=
new
TaggedItem(a,'add','waiting',tgSearch.currentSearch);




tgSearch.taggedItems.push(t);


}




addTaggedItem(t);






submitAddTag(t);
}

/*

Success
handler
for
addTag.

Updates
the
"you've
tagged
x
products
count
by

incrementing,
as
relying
on
the
TaggingService
to
return
that
count
in
a
transactional

way
turns
out
to
be
a
bad
idea.
*/
addTagResults
=
function(t,tagCountString){


if(t.status
!=
'error'){




t.action
=
'added';




tgSearch.searchResultsByASIN[t.ASIN.asin].status
=
'tagged';




displaySearchResults(tgSearch.currentPage,0);


}else{




t.status
=
'adderr';




updateTaggedItem(t);




return;


}
































































































































































if(tagCountString
!=
''){




updateTagCount(tagCountString);


}



updateTaggedItem(t);


jQuery("#taggedItemsDiv").scrollTop
=
0;
}

/*

Update
your
tag
count
with
the
given
string
*/
updateTagCount
=
function(tagCountString){


jQuery("#tgSearchTagCount").html(tagCountString);
}































































































































































/*

Remove
your
tag
from
an
item
*/
removeTag
=
function(asin){


t
=
tgSearch.taggedItemsByASIN[asin];
































































































































































t.status
=
'waiting';


t.action
=
'remove';


updateTaggedItem(t);





submitRemoveTag(t);
}

/*

Reveals
the
search
results
pane
*/
showSearchResults
=
function(){


var
divsToShow
=
['tgSearchTitle','tgQueueTitle','tgSearchResultsContainer','tgQueueContainer'];


for(var
div=0;div<divsToShow.length;div++){




jQuery("#"
+
divsToShow[div]).removeClass('tgSearchHidden');


}
}

/*

Hides
the
search
results
pane
*/
hideSearchResults
=
function(){


var
divsToShow
=
['tgSearchTitle','tgQueueTitle','tgSearchResultsContainer','tgQueueContainer'];
































































































































































for(var
div=0;div<divsToShow.length;div++){




jQuery("#"
+
divsToShow[div]).addClass('tgSearchHidden');


}
}

/*

Clears
the
search
input
box
*/
clearSearchField
=
function(){


if(tgSearch.searchFieldClicked){




return;


}


jQuery("#tgSearchValue").select().attr("class","").addClass("tgSearchBlack");


tgSearch.searchFieldClicked
=
1;
}
})(jQuery);
//-->
</script>
